### [281] [RotorMap and Quantum Fingerprints of DNA Sequences via Rotary Position Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22245)
*Danylo Yakymenko,Maksym Chernyshev,Illia Savchenko,Sergii Strelchuk*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于RoPE的量子编码方法，用于DNA序列比对，在经典计算中实现50-700倍加速，并在量子设备上验证了其可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA序列比对是生物信息学中的核心问题，传统方法如Minimap2在处理大规模基因组时计算成本高。量子计算为加速此类问题提供了新可能，但需要设计适合DNA序列的量子编码方法。

Method: 1. 基于Rotary Position Embeddings (RoPE)设计量子编码，将DNA序列映射到量子态
2. 经典版本：RotorMap算法，GPU加速的DNA映射算法
3. 量子版本：Angular编码，直接生成量子态制备电路
4. 在Quantinuum量子计算机（56-qubit H2-1, H2-2和98-qubit Helios-1）上进行实验验证

Result: 1. RotorMap在人类和玉米基因组测试中比单线程Minimap2快50-700倍
2. 量子编码在Levenshtein编辑距离和量子态保真度之间建立了强相关性
3. 在真实量子设备上成功验证了编码方法的可行性
4. 提出了量子DNA认证应用，可能在一方通信复杂度上实现量子优势

Conclusion: 该研究展示了RoPE编码在DNA序列量子处理中的有效性，为量子生物信息学提供了新工具，并指出了在DNA认证等应用中实现量子优势的潜力。

Abstract: For strings of letters from a small alphabet, such as DNA sequences, we present a quantum encoding that empirically provides a strong correlation between the Levenshtein edit distance and the fidelity between quantum states defined by the encodings. It is based on the principles of Rotary Position Embeddings (RoPE), employed in modern large language models. Classically, this encoding yields RotorMap - a GPU-accelerated DNA mapping algorithm that achieves speedups of 50-700x over single-thread Minimap2 in proof-of-concept tests on human and maize genomes. For use on quantum devices, we introduce the Angular encoding, which is built from RoPE and directly outputs state preparation circuits. To verify its properties and utility on NISQ devices, we report results of experiments conducted on quantum computers from Quantinuum: the 56-qubit H2-1, H2-2 and the latest 98-qubit Helios-1. As a potential application, we consider a quantum DNA authentication problem and conjecture that a quantum advantage in one-way communication complexity could be achieved over any comparable classical solution.

</details>


### [282] [Polymer identification via undetected photons using a low footprint nonlinear interferometer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22253)
*Atta Ur Rehman Sherwani,Emma Pearce,Philipp Hildenstein,Felix Mauerhoff,Alexander Sahm,Katrin Paschke,Helen M. Chrzanowski,Sven Ramelow*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 开发了一种紧凑型非线性干涉仪，用于快速检测塑料污染，无需中红外技术即可获取塑料特征吸收光谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 塑料污染已成为全球性挑战，微塑料广泛存在于生态系统和人类食物链中。现有拉曼和FTIR光谱技术难以实现快速、可靠、便携的材料识别，需要一种新的现场部署解决方案。

Method: 采用非线性干涉仪中的未检测光子光谱技术，通过仅检测近红外信号光子来获取中红外吸收光谱。开发了高度紧凑、微集成、热稳定的Michelson型非线性干涉仪，用于塑料快速光谱分析。

Result: 在室温下实现了34的信噪比、100 Hz的测量速率和6 cm⁻¹的光谱分辨率。能够准确快速地获取聚丙烯、聚乙烯、聚苯乙烯等常见聚合物的特征振动吸收光谱，无需使用中红外技术。

Conclusion: 该紧凑模块为环境监测系统和其他中红外光谱应用提供了一个有前景的现场部署平台，可实现稳健的实时监测。

Abstract: Plastic pollution has become a critical global challenge, with microplastics pervading ecosystems and entering human food chains. Effectively monitoring this widespread contamination demands rapid, reliable, and portable material identification techniques that often elude conventional Raman and FTIR spectroscopy. Undetected photon spectroscopy within a nonlinear interferometer (NLI) offers a solution, allowing the retrieval of mid-infrared absorption spectra by detecting only near-infrared signal photons using standard silicon-based technology. Here, we demonstrate a highly compact, micro-integrated, thermally-stabilised NLI with a Michelson-like geometry designed for the rapid spectroscopy of plastics. We benchmarked its room-temperature performance, demonstrating a signal-to-noise ratio of 34 with a measurement rate of 100 Hz and a spectral resolution of 6 cm$^{-1}$. We show that we can accurately and rapidly retrieve the characteristic vibrational absorption spectra of common polymers such as polypropylene, polyethene, and polystyrene, without using mid-infrared technology. These results establish our compact module as a promising field-deployable platform for robust, real-time environmental monitoring systems and other mid-infrared spectroscopy applications.

### [283] [Precision's arrow of time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.22284)
*Luis E. F. Foa Torres,G. Pappas,V. Achilleos,D. Bautista Avilés*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 论文提出"精度诱导不可逆性"(PIR)作为时间箭头的第三种机制，不需要量子退相干或混沌，仅需放大、非正规性和有限动态范围三个要素即可产生操作性的时间箭头。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上时间箭头归因于环境纠缠导致的退相干和混沌非线性动力学，但本文旨在探索是否存在第三条路径，不依赖量子纠缠或非线性也能产生不可逆性。

Method: 通过非厄米演化、放大和非正规性相互作用，结合有限动态范围，研究系统在超过可预测性时间界限后的行为。使用回声保真度测试验证理论预测。

Result: 发现存在一个与可用精度线性相关的尖锐时间可预测性界限，超过该界限后不同状态会坍缩到相同的表示中。回声保真度测试在任意精度计算和硬件中都证实了这一转变。

Conclusion: 精度诱导不可逆性(PIR)是时间箭头的一种新机制，揭示了形式可逆性与物理可逆性之间的差异，表明即使数学上可逆的系统，在有限精度下也会表现出不可逆行为。

Abstract: The arrow of time is usually attributed to two mechanisms: decoherence through environmental entanglement, and chaos through nonlinear dynamics. Here we demonstrate a third route, Precision-Induced Irreversibility (PIR), requiring neither. No entanglement. No nonlinearity. Just three ingredients: amplification, non-normality, and finite dynamic range, whose interplay yields an operational arrow of time; remove any one and reversibility can be restored. Non-Hermitian evolution remains mathematically invertible, yet beyond a sharp temporal predictability horizon scaling linearly with available precision, distinct states collapse onto identical representations. Echo-fidelity tests confirm this transition across arbitrary-precision calculations and hardware, revealing where formal invertibility and physical reversibility diverge.

</details>
